\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  For countries with higher mean average happiness at least
  \(\frac{2}{3},\frac{1}{3}-\frac{2}{3}\), less than \(\frac{1/3}\),
  what are the distribution for the three variables?
\end{enumerate}
